< Text>
They have great seasoned crinkle fries. The food came out nice and warm which was good. I got the Super Burger which had a good flavor. The staff was friendly through the drive thru. They have several selections to choose from. For a fast food burger place they are good. Would definitely go here over a burger king or jack in the box if they were closer to me. I wouldnt drive out of my way unless i had a taste for their fries. They toast the buns which is always a good play for a burger and the cheese was nice and melty the way In n Out does it. Reminds me of Flame It burger down on the south end of Chestnut.

Now that I'm typing the reviews it makes me want to try again so i will do that and potentially up the rating. They werent bad at all. Frozen patties but a good burger. If you are looking for something different it's worth a try with a decent variation of menu items. I took a few pics to help.<//Text>

< Text>
Decent food, really good for a drive-thru/fast food. The burgers are on par with Sonic or Whataburger. The "Super Sauce" is a mayo/mustard mix. I wasn't a big fan because I don't like mustard. But I could see it being a treat. They will grill your onions for your burger on request and that was super yummy. The fries are crinkle cut like Del Taco and seasoned with seasoning salt like Red Robin.
The chicken strips are mediocre. There is almost more batter than chicken and need sauce. The ranch dipping sauce is tasty, so don't forget that or ketchup. And they have that great small, slushy style ice like Sonic has, that kind is great for chewing.
Over all a good meal when you need a fast simple meal.< /Text>

< review>
My family and I received our covid vaccinations at Centinela hospital. As physicians, my husband and I were very impressed with the organization, professionalism, and the kindness of the staff. It feels more like a family when you walk in. Everyone was helpful and polite. Even the gardener greeted us !
The staff were competent and compassionate. Melba was not only gracious but oversaw much of the process. She is a super star!From check in to check out the whole process ran smoothly. Dr. Patel, the other doctors, nurses and entire staff should be very proud of their contribution to jumping into action when the vaccines first became available. It was seamless for patients. We are immensely grateful.<//review>

<time>1601758026312</time><rating>5</rating>< review>
This review is of the facility and hospital staff when you are there for other care outside of the Emergency Room.

I was very impressed with both their safety protocols upon entering the hospital building, the staff there to help direct you, as well as the staff in general admitting you and processing you for whatever reason you are there.

Had surgery there very recently, and with all the bad experiences I've heard of people having here in the past, I was prepared to lower my expectations and figured I would be in and out and let that be that. However I had a wonderful experience with the nurses and staff there. Everyone was so very attentive and caring and amazing, and I'm so very grateful.

I haven't used their ER in some time, and the last time I was there, half of them were fairly useless, the nurse even going against the proposed care plan the doctor had ordered for me, and another nurse fortunately attended to me (was dealing with necrotic tissue and a fever -- not good). However that was quite some years ago, and I do think they've turned things around since then. I'm happy to see the local community hospital is thriving and that our community can expect great medical care when needed.</review>
